SELECT c."CouponId", c."CouponCode", c."CouponDescription", c."CouponTypeId", c."CreatedAt", c."CreatedByUserId", c."DiscountValue", c."EndDate", c."IsActive", c."MinimumNumberOfUsage", c."MinimumOrderAmount", c."StartDate", c."UpdatedAt", s."CouponsProductId", s."AddedByVendorUserId", s."CouponId", s."CreatedAt", s."IsActive", s."ProductId", s."UpdatedAt", s."ProductId0", s."AddedByVendorUserId0", s."CreatedAt0", s."Description", s."MainProductSubCategoryAttributeId", s."ProductApprovalStatusId", s."ProductName", s."ProductStatusId", s."ProductSubCategoryId", s."UpdatedAt0", s."VendorId", s0."CouponUsageId", s0."CouponId", s0."OrderId", s0."UsedAt", s0."OrderId0", s0."AddressId", s0."CreatedAt", s0."FinalAmount", s0."OrderDate", s0."OrderNumber", s0."OrderStatusId", s0."TotalCouponAmount", s0."TotalProductAmount", s0."TotalShippingAmount", s0."UpdatedAt", s0."UserId"
FROM "Coupons" AS c
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c0."CouponsProductId", c0."AddedByVendorUserId", c0."CouponId", c0."CreatedAt", c0."IsActive", c0."ProductId", c0."UpdatedAt", p."ProductId" AS "ProductId0", p."AddedByVendorUserId" AS "AddedByVendorUserId0", p."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", p."Description", p."MainProductSubCategoryAttributeId", p."ProductApprovalStatusId", p."ProductName", p."ProductStatusId", p."ProductSubCategoryId", p."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0", p."VendorId"
    FROM "CouponsProduct" AS c0
    INNER JOIN "Product" AS p ON c0."ProductId" = p."ProductId"
) AS s ON c."CouponId" = s."CouponId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c1."CouponUsageId", c1."CouponId", c1."OrderId", c1."UsedAt", o."OrderId" AS "OrderId0", o."AddressId", o."CreatedAt", o."FinalAmount", o."OrderDate", o."OrderNumber", o."OrderStatusId", o."TotalCouponAmount", o."TotalProductAmount", o."TotalShippingAmount", o."UpdatedAt", o."UserId"
    FROM "CouponUsage" AS c1
    INNER JOIN "Order" AS o ON c1."OrderId" = o."OrderId"
) AS s0 ON c."CouponId" = s0."CouponId"
WHERE c."IsActive" AND c."StartDate" <= now()::timestamp AND c."EndDate" >= now()::timestamp AND c."MinimumOrderAmount" <= @totalCartAmount
ORDER BY c."CouponId", s."CouponsProductId", s."ProductId0", s0."CouponUsageId"
